[30;1m60 | [0m[35mCan PyVISA-py be used from a Docker container?[0m
[30;1m61 | [0m[35m----------------------------------------------[0m
[30;1m62 | [0m[35mAs the Windows variant of Docker can forward neither USB ports nor GPIB[0m
[30;1m63 | [0m[35minterfaces, the obvious choice would be to connect via TCP/IP. The problem of a[0m
[30;1m64 | [0m[35mDocker container is that idle connections are disconnected by the VPN garbage[0m
